msg:We chose Nanning Xinwei Marriott Hotel because it is a Marriott brand and because it is close to the Qingxiu Mountain Scenic Area where we are going. It is convenient to walk there. Metro Line 1 is also a few minutes away, and it is very convenient to go to the high-speed rail station and other places. The hotel's interior environment is relatively grand, and the front desk is enthusiastic and professional when handling formalities. The room decoration is simple and practical, the bed is very soft, and the bedding and toiletries are good. There are many varieties of breakfast, which will make it difficult to choose. The ingredients are fresh, and I especially like to eat soy milk and fried dough sticks, which are delicious and soft and crispy. The freshly cooked noodles and noodles are all special. Below the hotel is Hangyang City, which has restaurants of various flavors. There are also many small stalls on the roadside, selling milk tea, handicrafts, etc., which are very good to visit. In terms of management and service, the hotel does not have many tricks, nor does it ask for WeChat and good reviews. The staff always keep a distance from you, but you will not feel neglected. It is always reassuring to choose Marriott.
